Support

Product support included

What's Product Support?

In the event your product doesn't work as expected or you need help using it, Amazon offers free product support options such as live phone/chat with an Amazon associate, manufacturer contact information, step-by-step troubleshooting guides, and help videos.
By solving product issues, we help the planet by extending the life of products. Availability of support options differ by product and country.  [Learn more](/ps/product-support?ref_=dp_pls_support&ref_=dp_ret_policy)

Your transaction is secure

We work hard to protect your security and privacy. Our payment security system encrypts your information during transmission. We don’t share your credit card details with third-party sellers, and we don’t sell your information to others.  [Learn more](/gp/help/customer/display.html?nodeId=201909010)

## Sustainability features

Energy efficiency

## ECOLOGO

---

ECOLOGO certified products are made with materials that reduce environmental impact at one or more stages of their life cycle, from raw materials to end of life. An ECOLOGO certification indicates that a product has met environmental performance standards, which include criteria in some or all of the following categories: materials, energy, manufacturing and operations, health and environment, product performance and use, and product stewardship and innovation. Products are evaluated on the applicable criteria through testing and auditing.

[Learn more about this certification](https://www.ul.com/resources/ecologo-certification-program)

Safer chemicals

Made with chemicals safer for human health and the environment.

As certified by

ECOLOGO

How trade-in works

How trade-in works

![Upgrade and save](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_delivery.png)

1. Upgrade and save

Accept your estimated trade-in value, buy your new device at the current price, and receive your delivery.

![Prepare device](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_tell_us.png)

2. Prepare device

Sign out of all accounts linked to your old device, and factory reset it to erase your personal information.

![Ship within 30 days](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_send.png)

3. Ship within 30 days

Print your shipping label, [package your old device](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=G2Q9VNXJ29E7AK89), and drop it off at any UPS location within 30 days of receiving your new device.

![Get your rebate](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/2_how_rebate.png)

4. Get your rebate

After we receive your trade-in device, we'll verify it within 10 business days. Once verified, you'll receive your [trade-in value](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=GNESDAAB2JL84N3A) as an Amazon.com Gift Card to your Amazon account for immediate use.

# About this item

* Google Pixel 10 Pro XL is the ultimate Pixel experience, featuring advanced AI - Gemini, unbelievable camera quality, impeccable design, and the next-gen Google Tensor G5 chip[1]
* Unlocked Android phone gives you the flexibility to change carriers and choose your own data plan[2]; it works - Google Fi, Verizon, T-Mobile, AT&T, and other major carriers
* Pixel’s pro camera system makes everything look amazing, even in low light; capture more of the scene - advanced Google AI models, and bring out incredible details - 100x Pro Res Zoom, stunning 50 MP images, and super steady videos in 8K
* Pixel 10 Pro XL is built - durable aluminum and Corning Gorilla Glass Victus 2 for scratch and drop resistance; the 6.8-inch Super Actua display - 3,300-nit peak brightness is easy on the eyes, even in direct sunlight[3]
* Instead of typing, use Gemini Live to have a natural, free-flowing conversation; point your camera at what you’re curious about – like a sea creature at the aquarium – or chat - Gemini to brainstorm ideas or get things done across apps[4]

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say

Customers find this phone to be the best Android phone of 2025, praising its amazing camera system, incredible screen, and responsive performance. The design receives positive feedback for its appearance and color, while the battery life and value for money receive mixed reviews - some find it outstanding while others consider it not worth the flagship price. The phone's performance receives mixed feedback, with some saying it performs as advertised while others report it fails at basic tasks.

Amazon Customer

*5 out of 5 stars*

##### My favorite Phone! Just need a sims tray!

I'll start off by saying I wasn't planning on getting this phone at all. I've never owned a pixel before. But the moment I saw the reviews coming in about this phone and it's amazing features. They got me. And the fact that the prime sale had this phone marked down even more. The universe was telling me to get this phone. So I did and I couldn't be happier. To start they were right about the brightness of the screen. If you are out in the sun this phone will over power the suns light. If you don't have auto brightness on when you go to bed. I wish you luck for that flash bang that you are about to experience. One thing I wish I did was get the smaller pro. I have the XL and I feel like it's too big for my hands. Like it fits and I can hold it, but I'm a fan of skinny or tiny phones. This phone fits in my pockets. But from how big it is. You will know the moment your phone goes missing. Sounds quality is pretty good and they let you use spiral sound. And I know I've heard people complaining about the battery but I can make it through 2-3 days of use before needed to recharge. And that's without the battery saving mode. I use my phone alot but I don't play games on it very often. But when I do it doesn't get hot like my old phone would to the moment I booted up the same game. My hands would start burning. I also love the features this phone has. The voice callinf assistance that will answer spam calls for you or strange numbers to see if they are real or spam. Let the phone make notes during your important calls so you don't forget what the other person told you. The auto 911 calling feature if you get into a crash the phone will call the police and let you know that you need help without your having to say a word. This phone is packed to the brim with amazing features and I love it. They also give you free access to their VPN and YouTube premium for 3 months. Amazing value for the money. And last but not least the camera quality is fantastic. I be taking pictures of everything and everything comes out crystal clear. 50mp, HDR, high resolution pictures. My only cons are. Please bring back the physical sims tray and expandable memory. This phone like them all nowadays comes with no charging brick or headphone jack. And if you use the IR blaster you won't find it here. I don't use it but wanted to warn others incase you do.

  ##### [*5.0 out of 5 stars* My First Week with the Pixel 10 Pro: It's Scarily Smart](/gp/customer-reviews/R1MWTTZ1287BEW/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

  Reviewed in the United States on October 3, 2025

  Color: MoonstoneSize: 128GBStyle: Pixel 10 Pro (Phone Only)[Verified Purchase](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

  Alright, so I’ve had the new Pixel 10 Pro for about a week now, and I’ve finally gathered my thoughts. Let me just say, this thing feels less like a phone and more like some gadget from a sci-fi movie.
  First off, taking it out of the box, it just feels premium. It has a nice weight to it—not too heavy, but it feels solid and well-built. The matte finish on the back is a lifesaver for someone like me who hates fingerprints. The screen is the real star, though. It’s a big 6.7-inch display, and everything just looks incredible on it. Scrolling is buttery smooth, and watching videos is a treat. It’s super bright too, so I had no trouble seeing it outside, even in the afternoon sun.
  But let's be real, you buy a Pixel for the camera, and this one is just insane. I took it out over the weekend, and I’m blown away. The main camera takes ridiculously sharp and colorful photos without you having to do anything. But the feature I can't stop playing with is the "Pro Res Zoom." I was at a park and saw a cool bird way up in a tree. Normally, that would just be a blurry mess on my old phone. With this, I zoomed all the way in, and the photo is actually sharp enough to see the details on its feathers. It feels like magic.
  Google's AI stuff is all over this phone. They have this new feature called "Magic Cue" that tries to guess what you need. At first, it was a little weird, but now I’m getting used to it. Like, when I was heading to a meeting, it popped up a notification with the address and traffic info without me even asking. Another fun one is "Nano Banana"—silly name, I know—but it's this cool photo effect tool that lets you create some really artistic shots. Some of the results are a bit out there, but it's genuinely fun to mess around with.
  Performance-wise, it's a beast. The new Tensor G5 chip makes everything feel instant. Apps open right away, and I haven't seen a single stutter, even when I'm jumping between a bunch of different apps. The battery life has been solid too. I'm a pretty heavy user—lots of photos, social media, and some videos—and I've been easily getting through a full day with some juice to spare.
  So, is it worth it? It’s definitely not cheap, but if you're someone who loves taking pictures and wants a phone that feels like it’s one step ahead of you, I'd say absolutely. The Pixel 10 Pro isn't just a phone with a great camera; it’s a genuinely smart device that makes everyday tasks a little bit easier and a lot more fun. I'm still discovering new things it can do, and I'm honestly excited to see what else I find

  *5.0 out of 5 stars*

  ##### My First Week with the Pixel 10 Pro: It's Scarily Smart

  Reviewed in the United States on October 3, 2025

  Alright, so I’ve had the new Pixel 10 Pro for about a week now, and I’ve finally gathered my thoughts. Let me just say, this thing feels less like a phone and more like some gadget from a sci-fi movie.
  First off, taking it out of the box, it just feels premium. It has a nice weight to it—not too heavy, but it feels solid and well-built. The matte finish on the back is a lifesaver for someone like me who hates fingerprints. The screen is the real star, though. It’s a big 6.7-inch display, and everything just looks incredible on it. Scrolling is buttery smooth, and watching videos is a treat. It’s super bright too, so I had no trouble seeing it outside, even in the afternoon sun.
  But let's be real, you buy a Pixel for the camera, and this one is just insane. I took it out over the weekend, and I’m blown away. The main camera takes ridiculously sharp and colorful photos without you having to do anything. But the feature I can't stop playing with is the "Pro Res Zoom." I was at a park and saw a cool bird way up in a tree. Normally, that would just be a blurry mess on my old phone. With this, I zoomed all the way in, and the photo is actually sharp enough to see the details on its feathers. It feels like magic.
  Google's AI stuff is all over this phone. They have this new feature called "Magic Cue" that tries to guess what you need. At first, it was a little weird, but now I’m getting used to it. Like, when I was heading to a meeting, it popped up a notification with the address and traffic info without me even asking. Another fun one is "Nano Banana"—silly name, I know—but it's this cool photo effect tool that lets you create some really artistic shots. Some of the results are a bit out there, but it's genuinely fun to mess around with.
  Performance-wise, it's a beast. The new Tensor G5 chip makes everything feel instant. Apps open right away, and I haven't seen a single stutter, even when I'm jumping between a bunch of different apps. The battery life has been solid too. I'm a pretty heavy user—lots of photos, social media, and some videos—and I've been easily getting through a full day with some juice to spare.
  So, is it worth it? It’s definitely not cheap, but if you're someone who loves taking pictures and wants a phone that feels like it’s one step ahead of you, I'd say absolutely. The Pixel 10 Pro isn't just a phone with a great camera; it’s a genuinely smart device that makes everyday tasks a little bit easier and a lot more fun. I'm still discovering new things it can do, and I'm honestly excited to see what else I find

  ##### [*5.0 out of 5 stars* The Pixel 10 Pro XL is the best phone I have used in years](/gp/customer-reviews/R37R5XLYGEV1W2/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

  Color: MoonstoneSize: 256GBStyle: Pixel 10 Pro XL (Phone Only)[Verified Purchase](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

  I have owned many high-end phones over the years, but the Pixel 10 Pro XL in the 256GB Moonstone version is the first one I genuinely do not want to put down. After two weeks of heavy daily use that includes photo editing on the go, 4K video calls, and constant work sessions with Gemini, it has already exceeded my expectations.

  The 6.8 inch Actua Display is excellent. The 120Hz refresh rate makes every swipe feel smooth, and the colors are vibrant enough to make Netflix and YouTube feel almost cinematic. The Tensor G5 chip combined with 16GB of RAM handles real multitasking with ease. I can edit RAW photos in Lightroom while listening to podcasts and the phone stays fast and responsive. The 5200mAh battery easily lasts through a full day of mixed use, and the included 45W charger brings it to about 70 percent in about thirty minutes.

  The cameras are another highlight. The long range zoom produces impressively clear images, and the AI support through Gemini offers helpful suggestions that consistently improve quick snapshots. Both the fingerprint sensor and the face unlock respond instantly. The IP68 protection handled an accidental splash without a single issue. WiFi 7 keeps my video calls stable, and the stereo speakers sound fuller than I expected for a phone of this size.

  After using many flagship phones over the years, this one feels different. It genuinely boosts productivity and day to day convenience. If you are upgrading from anything released before 2024, this is a phone that truly feels like a meaningful step forward. I have zero regrets so far.

  A slim protective case works perfectly with the XL size and keeps the grip comfortable.

2-Year Protection Plan  $73.99

2-Year Mobile Phone Accident Protection Plan

from Asurion, LLC

[3.6    2025](/product-reviews/B07P6YY1KL/ref%3Ddp_atch_dss_w_r_B09LNW3CY2_?ie=UTF8&showViewpoints=1)

* Coverage: Plan starts on the date of purchase. Drops, spills and cracked screens due to normal use covered from day one. Malfunctions covered after the manufacturer's warranty.
* Easy Claims Process: File a claim anytime online at www.Asurion.com/Amazon or by phone. Most claims approved within minutes. If we can’t repair it, we’ll send you an Amazon.com Gift Card for the purchase price of your covered product or replace it. A service fee will apply. $29 to repair or $49 to replace your phone.
* Product Eligibility: Plan must be purchased with a product or within 30 days of the product purchase. Pre-existing conditions are not covered.
* Terms & Details: More information about this protection plan is available within the “Product guides and documents” section. Simply click “User Guide” for more info. Terms & Conditions will be available in Your Orders on Amazon. Asurion will also email your plan confirmation with Terms & Conditions to the address associated with your Amazon account within 24 hours of purchase.

Complete Protect: One simple plan covers all eligible past & future Amazon Purchases

from Asurion, LLC

### Product Protection by Asurion, LLC

* Coverage: Plan starts on the date of purchase. Drops, spills and cracked screens due to normal use covered from day one. Malfunctions covered after the manufacturer's warranty.
* Easy Claims Process: File a claim anytime online at www.Asurion.com/Amazon or by phone. Most claims approved within minutes. If we can’t repair it, we’ll send you an Amazon.com Gift Card for the purchase price of your covered product or replace it. A service fee will apply. $29 to repair or $49 to replace your phone.
* Product Eligibility: Plan must be purchased with a product or within 30 days of the product purchase. Pre-existing conditions are not covered.

Support

Product support included

What's Product Support?

In the event your product doesn't work as expected or you need help using it, Amazon offers free product support options such as live phone/chat with an Amazon associate, manufacturer contact information, step-by-step troubleshooting guides, and help videos.
By solving product issues, we help the planet by extending the life of products. Availability of support options differ by product and country.  [Learn more](/ps/product-support?ref_=dp_pls_support&ref_=dp_ret_policy)

How trade-in works

How trade-in works

![Upgrade and save](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_delivery.png)

1. Upgrade and save

Accept your estimated trade-in value, buy your new device at the current price, and receive your delivery.

![Prepare device](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_tell_us.png)

2. Prepare device

Sign out of all accounts linked to your old device, and factory reset it to erase your personal information.

![Ship within 30 days](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_send.png)

3. Ship within 30 days

Print your shipping label, [package your old device](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=G2Q9VNXJ29E7AK89), and drop it off at any UPS location within 30 days of receiving your new device.

![Get your rebate](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/2_how_rebate.png)

4. Get your rebate

After we receive your trade-in device, we'll verify it within 10 business days. Once verified, you'll receive your [trade-in value](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=GNESDAAB2JL84N3A) as an Amazon.com Gift Card to your Amazon account for immediate use.

   ## Global Recycled Standard

   ---

   Global Recycled Standard (GRS) certified products contain recycled content that has been independently verified at each stage of the supply chain, from the source to the final product and meet social, environmental, and chemical requirements. The purchase of Global Recycled Standard (GRS) certified products supports the use of recycled content in the supply chain. A product must contain at least 50% certified GRS material to qualify for inclusion in Climate Pledge Friendly.

   ---

   ### Certification Number

   TE-00322009

## What is Amazon Renewed?

Amazon Renewed is your trusted destination for products that are inspected, tested, and refurbished as necessary to be fully functional.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11X1grO0K6L.png)

#### Quality you can afford

Amazon Renewed products offer an affordable option so you can save on the brands you love.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11m5NyTwLVL.png)

#### Products you can trust

All products have been professionally inspected, tested, cleaned, and refurbished as necessary by Amazon-qualified suppliers. Products are not certified by Apple.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/118nlf+F3RL.png)

#### Trusted coverage

Your purchase is eligible for Amazon Renewed coverage in conjunction with Amazon's Return Policy and the A-to-z Guarantee.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11MpO5lMksL.png)

#### Purchases with an impact

Your Amazon Renewed purchase extends the lifetime of this product and reduces electronic waste.

#### What should I expect to receive with my Amazon Renewed purchase?

All Amazon Renewed purchases will come with accessories equivalent to those that shipped in the box when new. These items may not be original but will be compatible and fully functional. Amazon Renewed products will be packaged in either original packaging or in a new and clean cardboard box.

#### Model Year

2021

#### In what condition can I expect my Amazon Renewed product to be?

Product will be restored to its original factory settings and will be in one of the following cosmetic conditions Premium, Excellent, Good or Acceptable. [Learn more](/gp/help/customer/display.html?nodeId=202089470)

Shop for smartphones, computers, laptops, tablets, home and kitchen appliances, game consoles, office products, and more. [Visit Amazon Renewed](/renewed)

## Product Description

The iPhone 13 features a 6.1-inch (155 mm) display with Super Retina XDR OLED technology at a resolution of 2532×1170 pixels and a pixel density of about 460 PPI with a refresh rate of 60 Hz and Dolby Vision HDR. Additional features include a dual-camera system, consisting of a 12MP F1.6 wide-angle and another 12MP F2.4 ultra-wide camera with True Tone flash and lens correction. Both rear cameras have larger sensors with improved light sensitivity and Dolby Vision HDR video recording, but only digital zoom and no optical zoom. The front-facing ultra-wide camera is a 12MP F2.2 one. The iPhone 13 video recording supports 4K videos at 60fps as well as 1080p video at up to 240fps. The iPhone 13 model is available in six colors: Midnight, Starlight, Product Red, Blue, Pink, and Green.

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say

Customers find the iPhone 13 like new, with excellent condition and brand new appearance. The phone receives positive feedback for its quality, value for money, and functionality, with many saying it works like new. However, battery life and functionality show mixed results - while some report 100% battery health, others experience poor battery life, and some units stop working. The phone's condition is generally good, with no scratches or damage reported.

I searched everywhere and was very skeptical and nervous. I read review after review on every single possible option. I bit the bullet and took a chance. The phone came today. I took it out of the box looked it over up and down for five minutes, trying to find a single blemish. The phone is literally perfect condition. Brand new not a single blemish in sight. Turns it on and got everything set up in a matter of minutes. His battery was at 100% even my own phone only is at 83. I couldn’t believe it! Everything is working great it was really easy to set up. It does come in just a cardboard box and not an iPhone box, but I had an old one laying around to put it in. So that my son could feel like he was getting a brand new phone. I couldn’t be happier with the purchase and it came in under 24 hours. We activated under a boost Mobile plan for unlimited $25 a month. Now we are over here debating on ditching T-Mobile and swapping out our own phones since the quality is so amazing and the price honestly you can’t beat it.

  This was a gift for our daughter on her 13th birthday, her first phone. The battery health was 95 percent, the body of the phone looked new, and it has worked perfectly for her so far. It was packaged well and shipped fast. The charge cord it came with was generic, but it works.

  The only reason I am rating it 4 stars rather than five is that the screen had a rather large smudge scratch. Fortunately, once a screen protector was placed on it, the scratch became difficult to see. Given that you pay more for a renewed premium product, I just don’t think the phone’s condition quite meets the promised standard.

  Even so, overall we are pleased with the purchase so far, and our daughter is happy with the phone. We may go the renewed premium route for our next child when he gets old enough because of this experience.

  While I would have liked a better percentage. I received exactly what they claimed in the description.

  No complaints at all.

  It has only been a couple days since buying. I am really happy with this purchase.

  While there was an “excellent”condition iPhone, same as this one. Which was also cheaper. I do not regret getting this “premium,” phone.

  It has a one year warranty with Amazon. Which you don’t get on anything in less condition.

  With it being shipped and sold by Amazon I felt that also was in my favour.

Get your estimated trade-in value

How trade-in works

How trade-in works

![Upgrade and save](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_delivery.png)

1. Upgrade and save

Accept your estimated trade-in value, buy your new device at the current price, and receive your delivery.

![Prepare device](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_tell_us.png)

2. Prepare device

Sign out of all accounts linked to your old device, and factory reset it to erase your personal information.

![Ship within 30 days](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/how_send.png)

3. Ship within 30 days

Print your shipping label, [package your old device](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=G2Q9VNXJ29E7AK89), and drop it off at any UPS location within 30 days of receiving your new device.

![Get your rebate](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/G/01/tradein/WIP/2_how_rebate.png)

4. Get your rebate

After we receive your trade-in device, we'll verify it within 10 business days. Once verified, you'll receive your [trade-in value](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html?ref_=hp_left_v4_sib&nodeId=GNESDAAB2JL84N3A) as an Amazon.com Gift Card to your Amazon account for immediate use.

## What is Amazon Renewed?

Amazon Renewed is your trusted destination for products that are inspected, tested, and refurbished as necessary to be fully functional.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11m5NyTwLVL.png)

#### Products you can trust

All products have been professionally inspected, tested, cleaned, and refurbished as necessary by Amazon-qualified suppliers. Products are not certified by Apple.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11X1grO0K6L.png)

#### Quality you can afford

Amazon Renewed products offer an affordable option so you can save on the brands you love.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/118nlf+F3RL.png)

#### Trusted coverage

Your purchase is eligible for Amazon Renewed coverage in conjunction with Amazon's Return Policy and the A-to-z Guarantee.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11MpO5lMksL.png)

#### Purchases with an impact

Your Amazon Renewed purchase extends the lifetime of this product and reduces electronic waste.

#### What should I expect to receive with my Amazon Renewed purchase?

All Amazon Renewed purchases will come with accessories equivalent to those that shipped in the box when new. These items may not be original but will be compatible and fully functional. Amazon Renewed products will be packaged in either original packaging or in a new and clean cardboard box.

#### Model Year

2023

#### In what condition can I expect my Amazon Renewed product to be?

Product will be restored to its original factory settings and will be in one of the following cosmetic conditions Premium, Excellent, Good or Acceptable. [Learn more](/gp/help/customer/display.html?nodeId=202089470)

Shop for smartphones, computers, laptops, tablets, home and kitchen appliances, game consoles, office products, and more. [Visit Amazon Renewed](/renewed)

#### What should I expect to receive with my Amazon Renewed purchase?

All Amazon Renewed purchases will come with accessories equivalent to those that shipped in the box when new. These items may not be original but will be compatible and fully functional. Amazon Renewed products will be packaged in either original packaging or in a new and clean cardboard box.

#### Model Year

2023

#### In what condition can I expect my Amazon Renewed product to be?

Product will be restored to its original factory settings and will be in one of the following cosmetic conditions Premium, Excellent, Good or Acceptable. [Learn more](/gp/help/customer/display.html?nodeId=202089470)

## What is Amazon Renewed?

Amazon Renewed is your trusted destination for products that are inspected, tested, and refurbished as necessary to be fully functional.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11m5NyTwLVL.png)

#### Quality you can afford

Amazon Renewed products offer an affordable option so you can save on the brands you love.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11X1grO0K6L.png)

#### Products you can trust

All products have been professionally inspected, tested, cleaned, and refurbished as necessary by Amazon-qualified suppliers. Products are not certified by Apple.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/118nlf+F3RL.png)

#### Purchases with an impact

Your Amazon Renewed purchase extends the lifetime of this product and reduces electronic waste.

![](https://m.media-amazon.com/images/I/11MpO5lMksL.png)

How customer reviews and ratings work

Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.

[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref%3Dcm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say

Customers find the iPhone to be in perfect condition, like new, with a 100% battery life and good value for money. They appreciate its appearance, noting it looks like new with brand new screen and case, and one customer mentions the speakers work great. The phone's functionality receives mixed feedback, with some reporting it works like new while others say it doesn't work properly. Similarly, the unlock status is mixed, with some customers confirming it's unlocked while others report it being locked. The scratch resistance also gets mixed reviews, with some customers reporting no scratches while others mention scratches on the screen.
